## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant Main as main()
  participant Dao as DaoGenerate
  participant CS as CurrentStage
  participant Conn as Connection
  participant DG as DaoGenerator
  participant FW as FileWriter
  participant APIReq as APIGatewayProxyRequestEvent
  participant APIRes as APIGatewayProxyResponseEvent
  participant Ctx as Context

  Main->>Dao: main(args)
  Dao->>CS: setStage(stage)
  Dao->>Dao: runEntity(stage,directoryBase,packageName,true)
  Dao->>CS: getEnitityConnection()
  CS-->>Dao: Connection
  Dao->>DG: generator(connection,packageName,value,schema,key)
  DG-->>Dao: tableConstruct
  Dao->>FW: new FileWriter(filename)
  FW-->>Dao: write/close
  Dao->>Dao: runShipment(stage,...)
  Dao->>Dao: runLocation(stage,...)
  APIReq->>Dao: handleRequest(input, Ctx)
  Dao->>CS: setStage(requestContext.getStage())
  Dao->>Dao: runEntity/runShipment/runLocation (writeFiles=false)
  Dao-->>APIRes: response.withStatusCode(200).withBody("Done")
  APIRes-->>Main: response
```
